  GROUP 41 — Rage Mechanics, Stale Conditions, NPC Identity, Location Fidelity
  Session: April 16, 2026
  Source: Jtest5 session analysis (turns 200–231)
================================================================================

  BUGS FIXED (8 root causes from Testing.JSON session analysis)

  BUG A: Rage activation — `featureUsed` handler did not set `raging` condition
  BUG B: Rage damage bonus — `resolveAttack` did not add +2/+3/+4 to damage
  BUG C: Rage resistance — auto-fixed by Bug A (turn-executor.ts code was
         already correct; it just never fired because `raging` was never set)
  BUG D: Stale `unconscious` condition — never auto-cleared when HP recovered
         or on long rest
  BUG E: Friendly NPC used as enemy — Captain Arlen's quest-giver ID was
         emitted in `encounterStarted.creatures` as a hostile combatant
  BUG F: Missing location for supply line mission — AI narrated new mission
         area at old burned camp; prompt rules strengthened
  BUG G: Quest rewards defaulted to {xp:0, gold:0} because `rewards` field
         was absent from the questsAdded JSON schema spec
  BUG H: Prefixed weapon names ("Finely-crafted Dagger") not matching canonical
         stats because normalizeWeaponKey stripped all separators

  --- ENGINE CHANGES ---

  [1] adventure-turn.ts — featureUsed handler (~line 2944)
      When Rage activates, push 'raging' to char.conditions so downstream
      mechanics (damage bonus, resistance) can detect the state.
      NEW CODE:
        if (changes.featureUsed.feature === 'Rage' && char &&
            !char.conditions.includes('raging')) {
          char.conditions.push('raging');
        }

  [2] adventure-turn.ts — hpChanges handler (~line 2690)
      After char.hp is set, auto-clear 'unconscious' if HP > 0.
      Handles the case where a character was knocked out and then healed.
      NEW CODE:
        if (char.hp > 0 && char.conditions.includes('unconscious')) {
          char.conditions = char.conditions.filter(c => c !== 'unconscious');
        }

  [3] adventure-turn.ts — NPC death paths (3 sites)
      Clear NPC conditions when alive=false is set via:
        - hpChanges combatant HP → 0 (~line 2704)
        - autoClose victory path (~line 2460)
        - encounterEnded victory path (~line 3202)
      The npcChanges handler already had this logic; these 3 paths were missing it.
      NEW CODE (added after npc.alive = false):
        if (npc.conditions?.length) npc.conditions = [];

  [4] adventure-turn.ts — sanitizeStateChanges encounterStarted block (~line 2040)
      After the creature name check, reject any creature whose id matches
      a known NPC with role quest-giver/merchant/ally/companion or disposition ≥ 0.
      This is the engine-level guard against Captain Arlen-class incidents.
      NEW CODE (inside the filter callback):
        const existingNpc = state.npcs.find(n => n.id === cr.id);
        if (existingNpc && (
          existingNpc.role === 'quest-giver' || existingNpc.role === 'merchant' ||
          existingNpc.role === 'ally' || existingNpc.role === 'companion' ||
          existingNpc.disposition >= 0
        )) {
          console.warn(...); return false;
        }

  [5] adventure-turn.ts — normalizeWeaponKey / fuzzy weapon matching (~line 1825)
      At the two call sites (weapon normalization, armor normalization), added
      an IIFE fuzzy fallback that splits the item name into words and tries each
      (last→first) against CANONICAL_WEAPONS / CANONICAL_ARMOR.
      "Finely-crafted Dagger" → splits → last word "dagger" → canonical match.
      Pattern:
        const exactKey = normalizeWeaponKey(item.weaponName);
        const canonical = CANONICAL_WEAPONS[exactKey] ?? (() => {
          const words = name.toLowerCase().split(/[\s\-_,]+/).reverse();
          for (const w of words) { if (CANONICAL_WEAPONS[w]) return ...; }
          return undefined;
        })();

  [6] combat.ts — resolveAttack (~line 688)
      Added getRageDamageBonus helper (+2 at L1-8, +3 at L9-15, +4 at L16+)
      and included rage bonus in totalDamageMod for melee attacks (!weapon.range).
      NEW CODE:
        function getRageDamageBonus(level: number): number {
          if (level >= 16) return 4;
          if (level >= 9) return 3;
          return 2;
        }
        // In resolveAttack:
        const rageBonus = (attacker.conditions?.includes('raging') && !weapon.range)
          ? getRageDamageBonus(attacker.level ?? 1)
          : 0;
        const totalDamageMod = abilityMod + magicBonus + rageBonus;

  [7] rest.ts — LONG_REST_CLEARABLE_CONDITIONS (~line 131)
      Expanded from just ['frightened', 'charmed'] to also clear:
      'unconscious', 'prone', 'stunned', 'paralyzed', 'poisoned'.
      Conditions like 'blinded', 'grappled', 'petrified' remain non-clearable.

  --- PROMPT RULE ADDITIONS (gm-context.ts) ---

  [8] buildStateExtractionPrompt AND buildSystemPrompt — questsAdded format
      Added "rewards": {"xp": N, "gold": N} to the questsAdded schema in both
      functions. The engine already read this field (line 2650) but the AI
      never emitted it because it wasn't in the schema spec.

  [9] buildStateExtractionPrompt — LOCATION ENFORCEMENT rule
      After the existing "NEW place → locationsAdded" rule, added:
        "LOCATION ENFORCEMENT: When a quest or mission sends the player to a
         distinctly-named new place not in KNOWN LOCATIONS, emit locationsAdded
         with a new unique id AND locationChange. Never reuse an existing
         location id for a different new place."
        "DESTROYED LOCATIONS: If ESTABLISHED FACTS mention a location was
         burned, ruined, destroyed, or abandoned, treat it as inactive.
         Do not use that id for new missions."

  [10] buildStateExtractionPrompt — ENCOUNTER NPC IDENTITY rule
       After the "Only use encounterStarted when EXPLICIT attack" rule, added:
         "ENCOUNTER NPC IDENTITY: Each creature in encounterStarted.creatures
          must use (a) a brand-new unique id, or (b) an existing NPC id ONLY
          if that NPC is at the party's location with hostile disposition.
          NEVER use a quest-giver/merchant/ally id as a hostile creature."

  [11] buildStateExtractionPrompt / buildSystemPrompt — QUEST REWARDS rule
       After the QUEST COMPLETION METHOD rule, added:
         "QUEST REWARDS: Every quest created via questsAdded MUST include a
          rewards object with non-zero xp (minimum 50 × recommendedLevel).
          Include gold when quest-giver is noble/officer/merchant.
          Never emit rewards: {xp:0, gold:0}."

  --- TEST CHANGES ---

  rest.test.ts — Two tests updated to use 'grappled' instead of 'poisoned'
  as the representative non-clearable condition, since 'poisoned' is now
  correctly cleared on long rest:
    Line ~655: 'does not remove non-clearable conditions'
    Line ~663: 'handles multiple clearable and non-clearable conditions'

  --- RESULTS ---

  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline):
    combat.ts:136, gm-context.ts(~1363), turn-executor.ts:913+1539
  Tests: 54 failed / 1439 passed — exactly at Group 40 baseline.

================================================================================
  GROUP 42 — Starting Equipment UI: Expandable Detail Panels, Weapon Picks,
             Armor AC, Pack Contents, Instrument Chooser, Full Inventory Wiring
================================================================================

  --- PROBLEM ---
  Character creation Step 5 showed equipment choices as plain text buttons only.
  Selecting "Martial Weapon" defaulted to longsword in inventory regardless of
  intent. "Two Martial Weapons" had no sub-selection UI. Armor showed no AC info.
  Packs showed no contents preview. Bard "Musical Instrument" placeholder was
  never resolved to a real instrument. Shield was treated as misc armor.

  --- SOLUTION ---

  Files modified: 4
    src/lib/game/data/equipment.ts
    src/lib/game/types.ts
    src/lib/game/character-creation.ts
    src/lib/components/CharacterCreation.svelte

  ── equipment.ts ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Added at end of file:
    export const INSTRUMENTS: string[] = [
      'Bagpipes', 'Drum', 'Dulcimer', 'Flute', 'Lute', 'Lyre',
      'Horn', 'Pan Flute', 'Shawm', 'Viol'
    ];
  Purpose: SRD instrument list used in Bard instrument picker UI.

  ── types.ts ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  CharacterCreateInput gains new optional field:
    equipmentSubSelections?: Record<string, string[]>
  Key format: "sub-{choiceIndex}", value = array of chosen display names.
  Example: { "sub-1": ["Longsword", "Greatsword"] } for "Two Martial Weapons".

  ── character-creation.ts ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Added module-level constants (after ALL_ABILITIES):
    WEAPON_PLACEHOLDER_NAMES: Set<string> — normalized placeholder labels
      ('martial weapon', 'two martial weapons', 'simple weapon', etc.)
    KNOWN_INSTRUMENT_NAMES: Set<string> — all SRD instrument names lowercase

  resolveStartingEquipment() — REWRITTEN to use sub-selections:
    OLD: flat-maps all selected option labels, passes to itemFromLabel.
         'Martial Weapon' always became 'longsword' via GENERIC_WEAPON_FALLBACK.
    NEW: iterates choice rows; for each label, if it is a weapon/instrument
         placeholder AND equipmentSubSelections["sub-N"] is non-empty, pushes
         the sub-picks array instead of the placeholder label.
         Falls back to placeholder (and GENERIC_WEAPON_FALLBACK) if user made
         no sub-selection.

  itemFromLabel() — EXTENDED before catch-all misc block:
    Checks KNOWN_INSTRUMENT_NAMES for instrument names like 'Lute', 'Flute'.
    Creates a misc item with:
      category: 'misc', tags: ['tool', 'musical-instrument']
      name: the chosen instrument name (e.g. 'Lute')
      weight/cost/description from getGear('musical-instrument') entry
    This also resolves Bard option[0] = ['Lute'] correctly (was previously
    falling through to generic "Starting equipment: Lute" catch-all).

  ── CharacterCreation.svelte ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  Imports added:
    import type { WeaponDefinition, ArmorDefinition, GearDefinition } from '$lib/game'
    import { WEAPONS, INSTRUMENTS, getArmor, getGear } from '$lib/game'

  Form state update — added to $state<CharacterCreateInput>({...}):
    equipmentSubSelections: {}

  New $state variables:
    openChoiceIdx: number | null  — which choice row's detail panel is open
    manuallyClosedSet: Set<number> — rows user has manually closed via caret

  Panel visibility rules (single panel open at a time):
    isPanelOpen(ci) = openChoiceIdx === ci && !manuallyClosedSet.has(ci)
    selectEquipmentOption(ci, optIdx):
      - If new row (ci !== openChoiceIdx): delete ci from manuallyClosedSet,
        set openChoiceIdx = ci
      - If switching option within same row: call setSubPick(ci, []) to reset
        sub-picks (prevents stale picks from a different option bleeding in)
      - Always calls setEquipmentSelection(ci, optIdx)
    closePanelManually(ci): adds ci to manuallyClosedSet (caret-close)
    syncEquipmentState(): now also resets equipmentSubSelections, openChoiceIdx,
      manuallyClosedSet when class changes

  Panel auto-open behaviour:
    - Selecting any option auto-opens a panel for that row (if there is detail
      to show — armor AC, pack contents, weapon list, or instrument list)
    - Only one row's panel is open at a time
    - Caret (▲) on an open panel manually closes it (pauses auto-open for that
      row until user clicks into a different row, then resets)
    - Clicking to a different row: previous panel closes, new panel opens

  New helper functions (all in <script> block):

    WEAPON_PLACEHOLDER_SET: Set<string> (same list as character-creation.ts)

    getWeaponPlaceholderInOption(option): string | null
      Returns first item name that is a weapon placeholder, or null.

    isInstrumentPlaceholder(label): boolean
      True when label.toLowerCase() === 'musical instrument'.

    getInstrumentPlaceholderInOption(option): string | null

    parsePlaceholderCount(placeholder): number
      Returns 2 for "Two X", 3 for "Three X", etc. (defaults to 1).

    getWeaponsForPlaceholder(placeholder): WeaponDefinition[]
      martial → WEAPONS filtered by category.startsWith('martial')
      ranged  → WEAPONS filtered by category.endsWith('-ranged')
      else    → WEAPONS filtered by category.startsWith('simple')

    weaponPrimaryStat(w): 'STR' | 'DEX'
      DEX for finesse or ranged weapons; STR otherwise.

    getArmorInOption(option): ArmorDefinition | null
      Returns first non-shield armor entry found in option array.

    hasShieldInOption(option): boolean
      Returns true if any item in option resolves to a shield-type armor.

    getPackInOption(option): GearDefinition | null
      Returns first GEAR entry with contents array.

    computeArmorAC(armor): { formula: string; total: number }
      Heavy (maxDexBonus === 0): baseAC only
      Light (maxDexBonus === null): baseAC + full DEX modifier
      Medium (maxDexBonus === 2): baseAC + min(DEX, 2)
      Reads previewAbilities.dex (reactive $derived).

    getSubPicks(ci): string[]     — reads form.equipmentSubSelections["sub-{ci}"]
    setSubPick(ci, picks): void   — writes form.equipmentSubSelections["sub-{ci}"]
    toggleSubPick(ci, name, max): — adds/removes one occurrence of name,
                                    allows duplicates up to max (e.g. 2× Longsword)

  Template — equipment choices block REWRITTEN:
    For each choice row, {@const} vars derived from selectedOption:
      armorEntry, shieldPresent, packEntry, weaponPH, instPH, pickCount, subPicks

    Option buttons:
      - Display: option.join(' + ') (unchanged)
      - Added pick-count-badge inside selected button when optPC > 1:
          "{subPicks.length}/{optPC}" (e.g. "1/2")

    Detail panels (shown inside {#if rowOpen}):

      Armor / Shield panel  {#if armorEntry || shieldPresent}:
        Shows: displayName, armor-type-tag (Light/Medium/Heavy),
               "AC {total} ({formula})" using computeArmorAC
        Shield-only: just shows shield-badge "+2 AC (Shield)"
        Caret button: closePanelManually(choiceIdx)

      Pack panel  {#if packEntry}:
        Shows: pack displayName + <ul> of packEntry.contents items
        Caret button: closePanelManually(choiceIdx)

      Weapon list panel  {#if weaponPH}:
        Shows header with placeholder name + pick-count-badge if pickCount > 1
        Each weapon as equip-weapon-row button:
          weapon.displayName | damage damageType · STAT [· range]
          weapon-count-badge (×N) if same weapon selected N>1 times
        Clicking row: toggleSubPick(ci, weapon.displayName, pickCount)
        Supports 2× same weapon or 2 different weapons for "Two X" cases.

      Instrument list panel  {#if instPH}:
        Shows 10 SRD instruments from INSTRUMENTS constant
        Each as equip-weapon-row button; single selection (radio-style)
        Clicking: setSubPick(ci, [instrument])

  New CSS classes added (after .equip-card.selected):
    .equip-detail-panel      — bg-alt background, subtle border, column flex
    .equip-detail-header     — flex row, space-between, for title + caret
    .equip-detail-row        — flex-wrap row for armor name/tag/formula
    .equip-detail-title      — flex row for panel title + badge
    .armor-type-tag          — accent-tinted pill, capitalize
    .ac-formula              — muted text for formula display
    .shield-badge            — accent-tinted pill for "+2 AC (Shield)"
    .equip-detail-caret      — bare button, muted chevron, hover=text
    .equip-pack-contents     — disc list, muted color, compact gaps
    .equip-weapon-list       — column flex, tight gap
    .equip-weapon-row        — full-width button, flex row, border
    .equip-weapon-row.selected — accent tint + border
    .weapon-name             — bold, min-width 120px
    .weapon-stats            — muted, DEX/stat info
    .weapon-count-badge      — ×N duplicate indicator, accent bold
    .pick-count-badge        — "N/Max" pill, accent, used in both option
                               buttons and weapon panel header

  --- KEY DECISIONS ---
  - Weapon sub-picks FULLY wired into inventory via equipmentSubSelections:
    Players who pick Mace get Mace. 2×Longsword stays 2×Longsword.
  - No default fallback when user has made a sub-selection (GENERIC_WEAPON_FALLBACK
    still used when no sub-selection is made).
  - Instruments resolve to a proper 'misc' tool item (not a generic catch-all).
  - Shield shown as a "+2 AC" badge only, not as full armor detail.
  - One detail panel open at a time across all choice rows.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline)
  Tests: 54 failed / 1439 passed — unchanged baseline


================================================================================
  GROUP 43 — Equipment UI Polish: Grid Layout, Tags, ×2 Glow, Shield Panel,
             Concrete Weapons, Apostrophe Fix, Unselected Default
  Files: equipment.ts, CharacterCreation.svelte
================================================================================

  --- MOTIVATION ---
  Group 42 left several rough edges:
    1. All option buttons started pre-highlighted (first option auto-selected).
    2. Shield appeared as an inline "+2 AC" badge inside the armor row rather
       than its own titled panel.
    3. Two-handed weapons were not visually incompatible with shields.
    4. No per-weapon tags (One-Handed / Two-Handed / Versatile / Ranged etc.).
    5. Weapon list had no grid alignment — name, damage, stat, properties were
       all free-flowing flex items.
    6. Clicking the same weapon twice could not reach "×2" (toggle removed it).
    7. Pack panels never appeared for Bard, Rogue, etc. due to apostrophe
       mismatch between classes.ts (straight apostrophe) and equipment.ts
       displayNames (Unicode curly U+2019).
    8. Concrete ranged rows (Light Crossbow + Bolts) showed no detail panel.
    9. Net had no "Restrains" note; its damage "0" showed as "0 bludgeoning".

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/game/data/equipment.ts
    * Added private normApost(s) helper that replaces U+2018 / U+2019 (curly
      apostrophes) with ASCII straight apostrophes before string comparison.
    * Updated getWeapon(), getArmor(), getGear() to use normApost() when
      comparing displayName against the query. This fixes Bard / Rogue pack
      panels that were silently returning null for "Diplomat's Pack" (straight
      apostrophe from classes.ts) vs "Diplomat\u2019s Pack" (curly in data).

  FILE: src/lib/components/CharacterCreation.svelte
    Script changes:
      · Added getWeapon to imports from '$lib/game'.
      · syncEquipmentState(): removed ?? 0 default; always resets all slots
        to -1 so the player must consciously choose each option.
      · selectEquipmentOption(): prevOptIdx defaults to ?? -1 (was ?? 0).
      · toggleSubPick(): Rewritten to allow duplicate picks. Previous logic
        always removed if present. New logic: if item already in list AND list
        is at capacity, remove one instance; if under capacity, always add
        (enables clicking same weapon twice to reach ×2).
      · New helper isWeaponTwoHanded(w): returns w.properties.includes('two-handed').
      · New helper getWeaponDisplayTags(w): returns ordered tag array:
          handedness tag first (Two-Handed | Versatile | One-Handed),
          then Ranged, Heavy, Light, Reach, Finesse, Thrown, Loading, Ammo.
          Ranged detection: w.category.endsWith('-ranged').
      · New helper getConcreteWeaponsInOption(option): iterates option items,
          skips weapon placeholders and instrument placeholders, calls getWeapon(),
          handles word-quantity prefixes ("Two Shortswords" → Shortsword via
          prefix strip + optional trailing-s removal). Returns unique WeaponDefinition[].
      · New helper concreteWeaponCount(weapon, option): returns how many times a
          specific weapon appears in an option (handles "Two Shortswords" → 2).
      · New helper subPicksContainTwoHanded(ci): returns true if any sub-pick
          item for choice ci resolves to a two-handed weapon.

    Template — full equipment block replaced:
      · selectedOptIdx defaults to ?? -1 (was ?? 0).
      · Added {@const selectedOption = selectedOptIdx >= 0 ? ... : []}.
      · Added {@const concreteWeapons = getConcreteWeaponsInOption(selectedOption)}.
      · Armor panel and Shield panel are now SEPARATE divs:
          - Armor panel: shows displayName, type tag, AC formula.
          - Shield panel: shows "Shield" heading, armor-type-tag "Shield",
            "+2 AC bonus · Requires one free hand" note, and a
            two-handed-warning paragraph when subPicksContainTwoHanded() is true.
      · New "Weapons Included" read-only panel for concrete weapon options
          (when concreteWeapons.length > 0 && !weaponPH && !instPH).
          Uses same 4-column grid with wCount ×N badge but no click interactions.
      · Weapon list grid: .weapon-header-row + column spans
          wcol-name | wcol-damage | wcol-stat | wcol-tags
          grid-template-columns: 2fr 1.4fr 0.5fr 2.4fr
      · Damage cell: shows "— (damage-none italic)" for net (damage==='0');
          shows "1d6 <muted damageType>" otherwise.
      · weapon-sel-badge: circular accent badge with "✓" for single pick;
          "×N" with glow (weapon-sel-double) for duplicate picks.
      · Two-handed conflict: equip-weapon-row.hands-conflict (opacity 0.45)
          when isWeaponTwoHanded(weapon) && shieldPresent.
          tag-conflict CSS applied to Two-Handed tag in same condition.
      · Net special note: "Restrains · DC 10 STR" tag-special pill.
      · weapon.notes rendered as tag-special pill for other special weapons.
      · versatileDamage shown as "(1d8 2H)" pill when present.
      · Instrument list preserved; now uses same 4-column grid with CHA stat
          and "Instrument" tag pill.

    CSS — old weapon styles replaced, new grid styles added:
      · Removed: .shield-badge, .weapon-name, .weapon-stats, .weapon-count-badge.
      · .equip-weapon-list: flex column, gap 0.15rem.
      · .weapon-header-row, .equip-weapon-row: display grid,
          grid-template-columns: 2fr 1.4fr 0.5fr 2.4fr, gap 0.45rem.
      · .weapon-header-row: muted uppercase label row.
      · .equip-weapon-row.readonly: no pointer-events, transparent bg/border.
      · .equip-weapon-row.hands-conflict: opacity 0.45.
      · .equip-instrument-list overrides grid columns to 2fr 0.6fr 0.5fr 1.5fr.
      · .weapon-sel-badge: circular accent, white text, inline-flex.
      · .weapon-sel-badge.weapon-sel-double: border-radius 8px, glow box-shadow.
      · .weapon-tag: small pill, bg-alt, border, 0.68rem text.
      · .tag-two-handed: accented border/color.
      · .tag-conflict: red tint background + border + text.
      · .tag-special: italic, muted.
      · .damage-type: muted text for damageType label.
      · .damage-none: muted italic for "—".
      · .two-handed-warning: #e05555 color, 0.78rem.
      · .wcol-name/damage/stat/tags: grid cell helpers.

  --- KEY DECISIONS ---
  - All option buttons start UNSELECTED (-1). No default auto-pick.
  - Shield always gets its own dedicated panel (not merged with armor).
  - "Weapons Included" panel (read-only) appears for concrete-weapon rows like
    [Light Crossbow, Bolts (20)] so players can still inspect properties.
  - Two-handed×shield conflict is visual-only (opacity fade + tag-conflict);
    it does not block selection so GMs can override.
  - Net damage='0' → shows "—" in damage column (accurate: net deals no damage).
  - Duplicate weapon picks use a glow badge; single picks use a checkmark.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline)
  Tests: unchanged baseline (UI-only changes)


================================================================================
  GROUP 44 — Equipment UI Refinements: Tag Colors, Sorting, Special: Row,
             Shield Text, ×2 Cycle, No Conflict Shading
  Files: CharacterCreation.svelte
================================================================================

  --- MOTIVATION ---
  After Group 43, several UX issues remained:
    1. Two-handed weapon rows dimmed when a shield was in the same option.
       Players should not be dissuaded from choosing a two-handed weapon as
       a starting item even if a shield is part of the same option bundle.
    2. Weapon list ordering was arbitrary (SRD data order).
    3. Versatile damage and special weapon notes were shown as inline tag pills
       instead of dedicated explanatory text.
    4. Shield description said "Requires one free hand" — unclear.
    5. Weapon property tags had no color-coding or hover explanations.
    6. The ×2 weapon cycle only went up (0→1→2) then single-clicked back down.
       User wanted: 0→1→2→1→0→repeat (full up-then-down pyramid).

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/components/CharacterCreation.svelte

  Script:
    · Added `let subPickDirections = $state<Record<string, 'up' | 'down'>>({})`.
      Tracks the current cycling direction per weapon per choice row.
      Key format: `"{ci}-{weaponDisplayName}"`.
    · syncEquipmentState(): Now also resets `subPickDirections = {}` when class
      changes or step is reset.
    · selectEquipmentOption(): When switching to a different option on the same
      row, filters out all `subPickDirections` entries whose key starts with
      `"{ci}-"` so directions are fresh for the new selection.
    · toggleSubPick() completely rewritten with direction state:
        - dir='up': adds an item if total budget has room, flips to 'down' when
          the new count reaches maxCount.
        - dir='down': removes an item, flips to 'up' when count reaches 0.
        - Stale 'down' at count=0 (option was reset): treats as fresh 'up'.
        - Budget-full + weapon not selected + going up: no-op.
        Sequence for maxCount=2: click1=×1, click2=×2, click3=×1, click4=×0.
    · Added `damageMaxValue(damage): number` — parses "XdY" → X*Y for sorting.
    · Added `DAMAGE_TYPE_ORDER` const: bludgeoning=0, piercing=1, slashing=2.
    · Added `sortWeapons(weapons)` — sorts by: (1) STR before DEX stat,
      (2) highest damageMaxValue first, (3) damage type order.
    · `getWeaponsForPlaceholder()` now calls `sortWeapons()` on its result.
    · Added `WEAPON_TAG_TOOLTIPS` const — maps tag name → short explanation
      string. Used as the native `title=` attribute on tag spans so the browser
      shows a tooltip on hover.
    · Added `getTagClass(tag): string` — returns CSS class for color-coded tags:
        Two-Handed→tag-two-handed, Ranged→tag-ranged, Reach→tag-reach,
        Finesse→tag-finesse, Versatile→tag-versatile, Heavy→tag-heavy.
    · Added `getWeaponSpecialText(w): string | null` — returns a combined string
      for versatileDamage ("Deals 1d10 damage when wielded with two hands.") and
      weapon.notes, or null if neither is set.

  Template:
    · Shield panel: changed +2 AC description from "Requires one free hand" to
      "Cannot be used with two-handed weapons."
    · Shield panel: removed `{#if subPicksContainTwoHanded(choiceIdx)}` warning
      paragraph (the "⚠ Two-handed weapons cannot be used with a shield" text).
    · Both weapon panels (concrete + placeholder):
        - Removed `{@const twoHandedConflict}` and `class:hands-conflict=` from
          button elements. All rows now render at equal opacity.
        - Added `{@const specialText = getWeaponSpecialText(weapon)}`.
        - Tag spans now use: `class="weapon-tag {getTagClass(tag)}"` and
          `title={WEAPON_TAG_TOOLTIPS[tag]}` (browser hover tooltip).
        - Removed inline tag pills for versatileDamage `(1dX 2H)` and notes.
        - Added `{#if specialText}` block below the wcol-tags span:
          `<span class="weapon-special"><em>Special:</em> {specialText}</span>`
          This span has `grid-column: 1 / -1` so it spans the full row width.

  CSS:
    · Removed `.equip-weapon-row.hands-conflict { opacity: 0.45; }`.
    · Removed `.tag-conflict { ... }` rule block.
    · Removed `.tag-special { ... }` rule block.
    · Removed `.two-handed-warning { ... }` rule block.
    · Updated `.tag-two-handed` to red tint (bg/border/text color #e05555).
    · Added color-coded tag rules:
        .tag-ranged   — green  (#4caf50)
        .tag-reach    — blue   (#2196f3)
        .tag-finesse  — purple (#ab47bc)
        .tag-versatile — yellow (#ffb300)
        .tag-heavy    — orange (#fb8c00)
    · Added `.weapon-special` rule:
        grid-column: 1 / -1; font-size: 0.72rem; color: var(--text-muted);
        border-top: 1px solid var(--border); margin/padding for spacing.
        em inside weapon-special: italic, var(--text) color for "Special:" label.

  --- KEY DECISIONS ---
  - No conflict shading: players should freely combine two-handed weapon with
    shield as a starting inventory choice (they can decide at runtime).
  - sortWeapons puts STR weapons first (higher typical damage), then DEX weapons,
    then within each group orders by highest max damage die, then damage type.
  - The ×2 cycle uses a direction Map so behavior is predictable regardless of
    how quickly the user clicks or switches between weapons.
  - Native `title=` used for property tooltips (no extra JS or DOM needed).
    Tooltips contain brief one-sentence explanations per property.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline)
  Tests: unchanged baseline (UI-only changes)


================================================================================
  GROUP 45 — Equipment UI: FIFO Weapon Eviction, Panel Toggle, One-Handed Tag
  Files: CharacterCreation.svelte
================================================================================

  --- MOTIVATION ---
  After Group 44, three UX issues remained:
    1. Clicking a new weapon when the budget was full did nothing (no-op). The
       player had no way to swap to a different weapon without manually removing
       the current one first.
    2. After manually closing a detail panel via the caret ▲, clicking the
       same option tab again would not reopen the panel.
    3. One-Handed tag used the default muted-text style; user wanted white
       background with black text to distinguish it visually.

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/components/CharacterCreation.svelte

  Script:
    · Removed `manuallyClosedSet` state variable entirely (no more Set of
      closed rows). Panel visibility is now purely: openChoiceIdx === ci.
    · syncEquipmentState(): Removed `manuallyClosedSet = new Set()` line.
    · isPanelOpen(ci): Simplified to `return openChoiceIdx === ci`.
    · selectEquipmentOption(ci, optIdx): Removed the manuallyClosedSet.delete
      logic. Now always sets `openChoiceIdx = ci` unconditionally so clicking
      any option tab always opens its panel, even if user had closed it.
    · closePanelManually(ci): Simplified to `if (openChoiceIdx === ci)
      openChoiceIdx = null`. Clicking the ▲ caret closes the panel; clicking
      the same option tab again re-opens it.

    · toggleSubPick() rewritten with FIFO eviction:
        - If the weapon is already picked (count > 0): runs the up/down cycle
          (same as before — cycle up to max, then down to 0, then repeat).
          If budget is full and direction is 'up', starts descending instead
          of being a no-op.
        - If the weapon is NOT picked:
          • If budget has room: adds the weapon normally.
          • If budget is FULL: evicts the oldest pick (`picks.shift()`) then
            appends the new weapon (`picks.push(itemName)`). Direction for
            the new weapon is set to 'down' if budget is now at max, 'up'
            otherwise.
        Examples (maxCount=2):
          • 1×Longsword + click Flail (room)    → 1×Longsword, 1×Flail
          • 2×Longsword + click Flail (full)    → 1×Longsword, 1×Flail
          • 1×Longsword, 1×Flail + click Blowgun→ 1×Flail, 1×Blowgun
          • 2×Greatsword + click Lance          → 1×Greatsword, 1×Lance

    · getTagClass(): Added 'One-Handed' case returning 'tag-one-handed'.

  CSS:
    · Added `.tag-one-handed { background: #ffffff; border-color: #cccccc;
      color: #111111; }` — white background with dark text.

  --- KEY DECISIONS ---
  - FIFO eviction preserves the player's most recent intent: the newest
    selection is always kept; the oldest is evicted.
  - Panel toggle is now a simple openChoiceIdx toggling: open on tab click,
    close via caret, re-open on next tab click. No separate Set needed.
  - Direction state (subPickDirections) per weapon is preserved across FIFO
    evictions so the up/down cycle memory is not lost on unrelated picks.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline)
  Tests: unchanged baseline (UI-only changes)


================================================================================
  GROUP 46 — Shield Description Fix + AI Narration Immersion Overhaul
  Purpose: Fix incorrect shield item description; redesign AI DM opening
           preamble and system prompts for full immersion — no quest spoilers,
           no NPC name dumps, no day-count leaks, no closing questions.
================================================================================

  --- RATIONALE ---
  Four problems were identified in the original AI narration behaviour:
    A. Opening preamble listed NPC names wholesale ("Mira, Torben, Aldric are nearby")
    B. Opening preamble named and described the first quest outright
    C. Opening preamble stated "It is Day 1, morning, under clear skies."
    D. Every AI response ended with "What do you do first?" / closing prompt
  Additionally, the shield inventory item had the wrong description ("A set of shield").

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/game/character-creation.ts
  -- itemFromLabel() armor description (line ~1148) --
    OLD: description: `A set of ${armor.displayName.toLowerCase()}.`,
    NEW: description: armor.name === 'shield'
           ? 'A singular shield, of wood and steel.'
           : `A suit of ${armor.displayName.toLowerCase()}.`,

  FILE: src/lib/game/world-bridge.ts
  -- armor() helper lambda description (line ~637) --
    OLD: description: `A set of ${name.toLowerCase()}.`,
    NEW: description: def?.name === 'shield'
           ? 'A singular shield, of wood and steel.'
           : `A suit of ${name.toLowerCase()}.`,

  FILE: src/lib/game/state.ts
  -- buildOpeningPreamble() — full rewrite --
    Removed: localNpcs listing (NPC name dump)
    Removed: quest.name + firstObjective announcement
    Removed: timeBeat string "It is day N, timeOfDay, under X skies."
    Removed: trailing "What do you do first?"
    Added: timeStr — time-of-day flavour sentence (dawn/morning/afternoon/dusk/night)
    Added: weatherStr — weather rider appended to timeStr when non-clear
    Added: feature row (unchanged — just the raw feature text, no "notable detail" preamble)
    Added: ambient quest hook system — 4 hook templates selected by stable hash of quest.id:
      [0] Town crier voice rising in the crowd — words half-heard, coin and trouble mentioned
      [1] Scrap of parchment skittering past the boot — large urgent letters, lost to the gutter
      [2] Child crying from a narrow alley — soft, persistent, unattended
      [3] Freshly posted notice on a nearby wall — ink still damp, small crowd reading
    Hook is chosen deterministically per quest so the same quest always generates the same hook.
    Quest name, description, and objectives are NEVER referenced.
    Escalation (if player investigates) is handled by the AI system prompt rules (see below).

  FILE: src/lib/game/gm-context.ts
  -- buildNarrativeSystemPrompt() --
    Removed: `End each response with a beat that invites the next player action.`
    Added:   === NARRATIVE STYLE === block (6 rules, see below) before buildGameStateContextBlock

  -- buildSystemPrompt() (legacy fallback) --
    Removed: `End each response with a beat that invites the next player action.`
    Added:   === NARRATIVE STYLE === block (same 6 rules) before buildGameStateContextBlock

  -- buildNarratorSystemPrompt() --
    Removed: `- End each response with a beat that invites the next player action.`
    Added:   === NARRATIVE STYLE === block (same 6 rules) after RULES section, before world knowledge

  -- buildGameStateContextBlock() TIME section --
    Added: `(Day count is for deadline tracking only. Do not reference day numbers in narrative output.)`

  -- buildNarratorSystemPrompt() TIME section --
    Added: same annotation as above

  UNIVERSAL === NARRATIVE STYLE === BLOCK (identical in all three prompt builders):
    - Write immersive second-person prose. Show the world; do not summarise it.
    - Do NOT end responses with questions or prompts that invite the player to act
      ("What do you do?", "Where do you go?", "How do you respond?" etc.).
      The player decides their own next move.
    - Do NOT list every NPC present in a location unprompted. Introduce names only
      when earned — when a character speaks up, steps forward, or is directly addressed.
    - Do NOT reveal quest names, objectives, or active leads in narration. Quests are
      discovered through play. Use ambient hooks only: a posted notice, an overheard
      fragment, a weeping figure in an alley. Never announce a quest directly.
    - Do NOT state day numbers in narrative text. Time of day and weather provide
      sufficient atmospheric context. Day numbers exist for mechanical deadline tracking only.
    - Escalation rule: if a player actively investigates an ambient hint (asks about the
      crier, picks up the flyer, approaches the crying figure), you MAY sharpen the
      detail. If they pursue it further, give them the full information plainly.

  --- DESIGN NOTES ---
  Quest discovery flow:
    1. Opening preamble: one ambient hook, stable per quest. Player may ignore it entirely.
    2. If player investigates: AI escalates — sharper detail, partial name, more words heard.
    3. If player digs further: AI gives full quest information plainly.
    4. Exception: if the player has clear prior knowledge (told by questgiver, knows the NPC),
       the AI may surface quest information directly — the rules say "never announce a quest
       directly", but if the player already has context, the AI can connect the dots.
  The NARRATIVE STYLE block is identical in all three prompt builders — universal, no variation.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc: 4 pre-existing errors only (unchanged baseline)


================================================================================
  GROUP 47 — Quest Discovery, Activation & Notification System
  Purpose: Fix the broken quest pipeline: quests added via questsAdded were
           hardcoded to 'available' and never surfaced in the player's journal
           or fired toast notifications. Also teaches the GM same-turn
           discover+activate pattern so reading a flyer activates the quest
           immediately. Adds a red dot badge on the Quests tab.
================================================================================

  --- RATIONALE ---
  Three disconnected layers were broken simultaneously:
    A. adventure-turn.ts broadcast 'game:quest-discovered' but never
       broadcast 'game:quest-update' for status transitions (accepted,
       completed, failed) — so the client had no signal to show a toast.
    B. +page.svelte imported toastQuestUpdate but had no socket handler
       for 'game:quest-discovered' or 'game:quest-update' — imported but dead.
    C. applyGMStateChanges hardcoded status: 'available' for all questsAdded
       entries; the GM prompt had no same-turn discover+activate pattern, so
       when a player reads a flyer the GM emits questsAdded but not
       questUpdates, leaving the quest invisible in the journal forever.

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/server/ai/adventure-turn.ts

  [1] broadcastTurnEvents() — add 'state: GameState' parameter
    OLD: async function broadcastTurnEvents(
           host: string,
           adventureId: string,
           resolvedTurn: ResolvedTurn,
           narrativeText: string,
           turnNumber: number
         ): Promise<void> {
    NEW: async function broadcastTurnEvents(
           host: string,
           adventureId: string,
           resolvedTurn: ResolvedTurn,
           narrativeText: string,
           turnNumber: number,
           state: GameState
         ): Promise<void> {

  [2] broadcastTurnEvents() — add quest-update broadcast block after questsAdded block
    Added after the existing questsAdded broadcast loop:
      // Quest status update events
      if (sc.questUpdates) {
        for (const qu of sc.questUpdates) {
          if (qu.field !== 'status') continue;
          const newVal = qu.newValue as string;
          const reason = newVal === 'active' ? 'accepted'
            : newVal === 'completed' ? 'completed'
            : newVal === 'failed' ? 'failed'
            : null;
          if (!reason) continue;
          const quest = state.quests.find(q => q.id === qu.questId);
          if (!quest) continue;
          await broadcastGameEvent(host, adventureId, {
            type: 'game:quest-update',
            adventureId,
            timestamp: now,
            quest,
            reason
          });
        }
      }
    Uses the post-apply state to look up quest names for the broadcast payload.
    The 'game:quest-update' interface already existed in events.ts (line 138).

  [3] First call site (~line 789) — pass currentState
    OLD: await broadcastTurnEvents(partyHost, payload.adventureId, finalResolvedTurn, narrativeText, turnNumber);
    NEW: await broadcastTurnEvents(partyHost, payload.adventureId, finalResolvedTurn, narrativeText, turnNumber, currentState);

  [4] Second call site (~line 1003) — pass state
    OLD: await broadcastTurnEvents(partyHost, adventureId, resolvedTurn, narrativeText, turnNumber);
    NEW: await broadcastTurnEvents(partyHost, adventureId, resolvedTurn, narrativeText, turnNumber, state);

  [5] applyGMStateChanges questsAdded block — respect optional status field
    OLD: status: 'available',
    NEW: status: (qData as Record<string, unknown>).status === 'active' ? 'active' : 'available',
    Allows same-turn discover+activate pattern: if questsAdded entry has status:'active',
    the quest is added in active state without needing a separate questUpdates entry.

  [6] sanitizeStateChanges questsAdded filter — sanitize optional status field
    Added after: if (typeof q.description !== 'string') q.description = q.name;
    Added:
      // Sanitize status — only 'available' and 'active' are permitted on new quests
      if (q.status !== undefined && q.status !== 'available' && q.status !== 'active') {
        console.warn([sanitize] questsAdded[N] "name" has invalid status="X" — forcing available);
        q.status = 'available';
      }
    Rejects 'completed'/'failed' on new quests (would be nonsensical).

  FILE: src/lib/game/gm-context.ts

  [7] buildNarrativeSystemPrompt() — QUEST ACTIVATION rule — add same-turn clause
    OLD (line ~193): - QUEST ACTIVATION: ... Activation requires clear, deliberate player engagement.
    NEW: appended SAME-TURN DISCOVER + ACTIVATE paragraph:
      "SAME-TURN DISCOVER + ACTIVATE: If the quest is brand-new this turn (you are
      also emitting it in questsAdded), include BOTH questsAdded AND questUpdates
      { field: 'status', oldValue: 'available', newValue: 'active' } in the same
      response — the engine applies questsAdded before questUpdates, so the quest
      exists when the activation fires. Do not defer activation to the next turn
      when the player already engaged the hook in this action."
    Same change applied to buildSystemPrompt() legacy prompt (~line 450).

  [8] buildStateExtractionPrompt() — QUEST ACTIVATION rule — add same-turn clause
    OLD (line ~577): - QUEST ACTIVATION: ... Do NOT activate quests for passive observation,
                      accidental overhearing, or casual proximity to a hook.
    NEW: appended same-turn variant:
      "SAME-TURN DISCOVER + ACTIVATE: If the narrative shows a brand-new quest being
      created AND the player engaging it in the same action, emit BOTH questsAdded AND
      questUpdates { field: 'status', oldValue: 'available', newValue: 'active' } —
      the engine processes questsAdded before questUpdates, so this is safe."

  [9] buildSystemPrompt() questsAdded JSON schema (~line 476)
    OLD: "questsAdded": [{"id": "quest-<unique>", ... "rewards": {"xp": N, "gold": N},
          "failureConsequence": ...
    NEW: optional "status" field added between rewards and failureConsequence:

    Same change applied to buildStateExtractionPrompt() schema (~line 639).

  FILE: src/routes/adventures/[id]/+page.svelte

      }
    Fires "Quest Discovered" toast label when the GM introduces a new quest into the world.

  [12] Add game:quest-update socket handler
    Added:
      if (msg.type === 'game:quest-update') {
        const questObj = (msg as any).quest as { name?: string } | undefined;
        const reason = String((msg as any).reason ?? 'accepted');
        toastQuestUpdate(questObj?.name ?? 'Unknown Quest', reason);
        if (reason === 'accepted') questNotification = true;
        invalidateAll();
      }
    Fires "Quest Accepted" / "Quest Completed" / "Quest Failed" toasts.
    Sets questNotification = true on 'accepted' to show badge dot on Quests tab.
    Calls invalidateAll() so the Quests tab data refreshes immediately.

    OLD: <JournalPanel ... worldCities={worldCities} />
    NEW: <JournalPanel ... worldCities={worldCities} bind:questNotification />

  FILE: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

    Added: questNotification?: boolean;

  [15] Props destructuring — make questNotification bindable
    Added: questNotification = (false),

  [16] Tab button onclick — clear badge when Quests tab opened
    OLD: onclick={() => activeTab = tab.id}
    NEW: onclick={() => {
           activeTab = tab.id;
           if (tab.id === 'quests') questNotification = false;
         }}

  [17] Tab button template — show badge dot when quest notification is pending
    Added inside each tab button (after tab-label span):
      {#if tab.id === 'quests' && questNotification}
        <span class="tab-badge" aria-label="New quest"></span>
      {/if}

  [18] CSS — tab-btn position + tab-badge styles
    Added:
      .tab-btn { position: relative; }
      .tab-badge {
        position: absolute;
        top: 0.3rem; right: 0.3rem;
        width: 0.5rem; height: 0.5rem;
        border-radius: 50%;

        0%, 100% { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1); }
        50% { opacity: 0.7; transform: scale(1.15); }
      }
    Red dot pulses softly; clears when the Quests tab is opened.

  --- DESIGN NOTES ---
  Quest pipeline (post-change):
    1. GM emits questsAdded (quest added to world state as 'available') →
       broadcastTurnEvents fires 'game:quest-discovered' → frontend shows
       "Quest Discovered" toast (ambient hook only, quest NOT in journal yet).

    2a. SAME-TURN PATTERN: GM emits questsAdded + questUpdates {→'active'} in
        same response (player read the notice, accepted from quest-giver) →
        broadcastTurnEvents also fires 'game:quest-update' reason:'accepted' →
        "Quest Accepted" toast + badge dot + journal updated.

    2b. NEXT-TURN PATTERN: In a later turn the player engages the hook →
        GM emits questUpdates {available→active} → same 'game:quest-update'
        broadcast → same toast + badge + journal update.

    3. Player opens Quests tab → badge clears → quest shown as Active.

    4. Quest objectives completed → auto-complete fires → questUpdates
       {→'completed'} → "Quest Completed" toast.

  Two-step architecture (questsAdded then questUpdates) remains canonical.
  Same-turn shortcut (questsAdded with optional status:'active') supplements it.

  --- RESULTS ---
  adventure-turn.ts: 0 errors
  gm-context.ts: 0 errors

================================================================================
  GROUP 48 — Inventory Overhaul: WU/SU Dual-Unit System, Drag-Drop Zones
================================================================================

  Purpose: Replace the flat inventory list with a 3-zone drag-and-drop layout
           using Weight Units (WU = 1 lb) and Space Units (SU = shape proxy)
           as dual capacity dimensions. Equipped zone has no hard cap but
           contributes to the global encumbrance bar. Containers enforce both
           WU and SU limits with animated rejection on overflow.

  --- RATIONALE ---
  The old inventory was a single flat list with no spatial logic. Items had
  weight but no shape/volume concept, containers had no enforced limits, and
  moving items between containers required manual GM narration. This group
  adds a complete SRD-informed dual-dimension system, location-based zones,
  and HTML5 drag-and-drop with optimistic UI + debounced PATCH persistence.

  --- KEY DESIGN DECISIONS ---
  - WU = 1 lb (1:1 with existing BaseItem.weight). No conversion needed.
  - SU (Space Unit) = shape/volume proxy. Coins ~0.01 SU; greatsword = 5 SU.
    Derived from ITEM_SU_TABLE lookup, fallback = max(0.5, weight x 0.7).
  - Equipped zone: shows all equipped===true items, contributes to total
    encumbrance bar, but has NO hard WU/SU capacity gate.
  - Containers zone: hard-cap drop when maxWU or maxSU exceeded =>
    shake animation + red invalid-drop-target glow. Move is rejected.
  - Loose zone: collapsible list of items not equipped and not in a container.
  - Encumbrance bar: 3 background zones (green/yellow/orange), threshold
    markers at 5xSTR (encumbered) and 10xSTR (heavily encumbered).
  - Atomic moves: remove-before-add, returns null on failure (UI reverts).
  - spaceTaken stored on item (computed at creation/load) to survive saves.

  --- CHANGES ---

  FILE: src/lib/game/types.ts  (Phase 1)

  [1] BaseItem.spaceTaken -- add optional SU field
    Added: spaceTaken?: number;
    Optional at creation; normalizeItem fills it in at load time.

  [2] ContainerType union -- expand with new container types
    OLD: 'backpack' | 'bag' | 'chest' | 'pouch' | 'saddlebag' | 'other'
    NEW: added 'belt-pouch' | 'coin-purse' | 'quiver' | 'belt' |
                'component-pouch' | 'scroll-case'

  [3] ContainerCapacity -- replace maxWeight/maxSlots with maxWU/maxSU
    OLD: { maxWeight?: number; maxSlots?: number; }
    NEW: {
      maxWU: number;           // hard cap in Weight Units
      maxSU: number;           // hard cap in Space Units
      discounts?: ContainerDiscount[];
      maxWeight?: number;      // deprecated -- migrated at load
      maxSlots?: number;       // deprecated -- migrated at load
    }

  [4] ContainerDiscount -- new interface
    export interface ContainerDiscount {
      category?: ItemCategory;
      nameMatch?: string;
      wuMultiplier: number;
      suMultiplier: number;
    }

  [5] EnhancedEncumbranceInfo -- new interface
    export interface EnhancedEncumbranceInfo {
      wuTotal: number;
      suTotal: number;
      capacity: number;                   // 15 x STR
      encumberedThreshold: number;        // 5 x STR
      heavilyEncumberedThreshold: number; // 10 x STR
      pct: number;               // 0-100+, capped at 120 for display
      isEncumbered: boolean;
      isHeavilyEncumbered: boolean;
      isOverCapacity: boolean;
    }

  [6] CharacterFeatureRef.tag -- add optional tag field

    Required by combat.ts Relentless Endurance check (pre-existing fix).

  FILE: src/lib/game/item-dimensions.ts  (Phase 2 -- NEW FILE)

    Examples: longsword=3, dagger=1, plate=10, coin=0.01, backpack=5,
              rope(50ft)=8, spell-book=3, healing-potion=0.5

  [10] CONTAINER_DEFAULTS -- maps each ContainerType to {maxWU,maxSU,discounts[]}
    Key values:
      backpack:        30 WU /  60 SU
      belt-pouch:       5 WU /  20 SU
      coin-purse:       5 WU /  20 SU  (coins: WU x 0.5, SU x 0.1)
      quiver:           2 WU /  20 SU  (ammunition: SU x 0.5)
      component-pouch:  3 WU /  15 SU
      scroll-case:      1 WU /   8 SU
      chest:          300 WU / 600 SU
      saddlebag:       60 WU / 120 SU

  [11] Exported pure functions:
    getItemSU(item)             -- SU lookup => stored spaceTaken => fallback
    getEffectiveWU(item, disc)  -- weight x discount multiplier
    getEffectiveSU(item, disc)  -- SU x discount multiplier

  --- DESIGN NOTES ---
  WU/SU duality:
    WU = lbs. Simple transport weight.
    SU = shape proxy. A 10lb boulder (SU 3) vs 10lb of coins (SU 0.10) --
    same weight, very different space. ITEM_SU_TABLE encodes SRD shape data.
    Fallback: max(0.5, weight x 0.7).

  Equipped zone has no WU/SU gate by design. The encumbrance bar still
  penalises overloading via total WU across ALL item locations.

  Container overflow rejection: canAddToContainer returns {ok:false}.
  handleDrop triggers @keyframes shake + red glow. Item snaps back visually.

  Backward compatibility: old saves with {maxWeight, maxSlots} are silently
  migrated by state.ts normalizeItem at first load. Old fields retained as
  deprecated on the type for database round-trip safety.

  --- RESULTS ---
  tsc --noEmit: 0 errors (all pre-existing errors also fixed)
  Files changed:  types.ts, state.ts, character-creation.ts, index.ts,
                  gm-context.ts, adventure-turn.ts, turn-executor.ts,
                  turn-executor.test.ts, JournalPanel.svelte
  Files created:  item-dimensions.ts,
                  routes/api/adventure/[id]/character/inventory/+server.ts


================================================================================
  GROUP 49 — Inventory Rebalance + Drag-Drop Overhaul
================================================================================

  CONTEXT
  -------
  Player-reported: characters became encumbered instantly on creation, and
  container drag-drop misfired due to false DragLeave events. No containers
  were created at character creation (backpack was stored as MiscItem).

  DESIGN DECISIONS (from 5-question user interview)
  --------------------------------------------------
  • Encumbrance thresholds: STR×15 = Loaded, STR×25 = Burdened, STR×30 = Overloaded
  • Worn/equipped items count at 25% WU toward encumbrance (body-supported)
  • SU displayed only inside container panels; NOT on main encumbrance bar
  • Containers auto-populated at character creation (two-pass routing)
  • Right-click context menu added as drag-drop fallback for touch/accessibility

  ── PHASE 1: Encumbrance Math ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/game/item-dimensions.ts

  getCharacterTotalWU() — worn item discount
    Items with equipped:true now contribute item.weight × 0.25 WU (not full weight).
    Container contents always contribute full weight (they hang from the body).

  getEnhancedEncumbranceInfo() — new thresholds
    OLD: capacity=STR×15, encumberedThreshold=STR×5, heavilyEncumberedThreshold=STR×10
    NEW: capacity=STR×30, loadedThreshold=STR×15, burdenedThreshold=STR×25
    Added: badge:'unloaded'|'loaded'|'burdened'|'overloaded' field

  CONTAINER_DEFAULTS — doubled standard container sizes
    backpack: 30WU/60SU  →  60WU/120SU
    sack:     15WU/30SU  →  30WU/60SU
    bag:      20WU/40SU  →  40WU/80SU

  ── PHASE 2: Type Update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/game/types.ts

  EnhancedEncumbranceInfo interface — renamed threshold fields + badge
    Removed: encumberedThreshold, heavilyEncumberedThreshold
    Added:   loadedThreshold, burdenedThreshold, badge
    Kept:    isEncumbered, isHeavilyEncumbered, isOverCapacity (semantics updated)
    Note:    isEncumbered now means wuTotal > loadedThreshold
             isHeavilyEncumbered now means wuTotal > burdenedThreshold

  ── PHASE 3: Container Capacities (covered in Phase 1 above) ────────────────

  ── PHASE 4: Auto-Populate Starting Containers ───────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/game/character-creation.ts

  Added imports: ContainerItem, ContainerType (from types), canAddToContainer,
                 getItemSU (from item-dimensions)

  Added CONTAINER_NAME_MAP — maps normalised item labels to ContainerType + weight:
    backpack → 'backpack' (5 lbs), sack → 'sack', bag → 'bag',
    coin purse → 'coin-purse', scroll case → 'scroll-case',
    component pouch → 'component-pouch', belt pouch → 'belt-pouch',
    quiver → 'quiver', pouch → 'belt-pouch'

  itemFromLabel() — detects container names before weapon/armor/gear lookup.
    Returns ContainerItem with capacity from CONTAINER_DEFAULTS when matched.
    Container items start with empty contents:[].

  resolveStartingEquipment() — two-pass algorithm:
    Pass 1: Build all items (containers get ContainerItem shape)
    Pass 2: Route non-equipped, non-container items into containers:
      ammunition  → quiver first, then backpack
      coins       → coin-purse first, then backpack
      scrolls     → scroll-case first, then backpack
      SU ≤ 1      → belt-pouch first, then backpack
      default     → backpack
      overflow    → stays loose (no hard fail)
    Equipped weapons + armor always stay as top-level loose items.
    Final order: containers first (filled), then remaining loose/equipped.

  ── PHASE 5: Drag-Drop Bug Fix ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

  handleDragLeave(e) — bounding-box guard added
    Old: cleared drop state immediately on any DragLeave event
    New: checks if the mouse is still within the drop zone's bounding rect;
         if cursor is still inside, the event is ignored (it was fired by a child).
         Signature changed from () to (e: DragEvent).

  ── PHASE 6: Right-Click Context Menu ────────────────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

  New state:
    contextMenu: { x, y, itemId, fromSource } | null

  New functions:
    handleItemContextMenu(e, itemId, fromSource) — fires on each item's
      oncontextmenu event; stores cursor position + item identity.
    closeContextMenu() — clears the state.
    moveViaContextMenu(toSource) — calls moveItemToContainer then
      onInventoryMove + persistInventoryMove (same path as drag-drop).
    $effect — installs a window mousedown listener to dismiss the menu when
      clicking outside; guards using .closest('.ctx-menu') to avoid self-close.

  oncontextmenu added to:
    • Equipped zone items (fromSource = 'equipped')
    • Container contents items (fromSource = container.id)
    • Loose zone items (fromSource = 'loose')

  Context menu HTML — fixed position at cursor, renders:
    • "⚔️ Equipped" (only for weapon/armor items not already equipped)
    • "🎽 Loose" (only when not already loose)
    • One button per container, disabled + "(full)" label when canAddToContainer fails
    • "✕ Cancel" at bottom

  ── PHASE 7: UI Cleanup ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  FILE: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

  Encumbrance bar zones — proportions now reflect actual thresholds:
    Green:  STR×0 → STR×15 = 50% of bar width
    Yellow: STR×15 → STR×25 = 33% of bar width
    Orange: STR×25 → STR×30 = 17% of bar width
    (Previously all three hardcoded at 33.33%)

  Encumbrance status labels renamed:
    OLD: Encumbered, Heavily Encumbered, Over Capacity
    NEW: Loaded, Burdened, Overloaded
    (Now driven by enc.badge field)

  Encumbrance popover text — updated thresholds + descriptions:
    Unloaded (0–STR×15): No penalty.
    Loaded (STR×15–STR×25): No speed penalty — but you feel the weight.
    Burdened (STR×25–STR×30): Speed −10 ft; disadvantage on STR/DEX/CON.
    Overloaded (>STR×30): Speed −20 ft; GM may impose further penalties.
    Note: "Capacity = STR × 30 WU. Worn/equipped items count at 25% WU."

  WU/SU popover text — SU role clarified:
    "SU does not affect the main encumbrance bar — only WU does."

  Item chips — SU removed from main inventory zones (equipped, container contents,
    loose). All chips now show only "{weight × qty} WU".
    Container load bars still show both WU and SU (per user requirement).

  --- RESULTS ---
  svelte-check: 0 new errors (18 pre-existing errors in AdventureCard.svelte,
    CharacterCreation.svelte, +page.svelte were unchanged)

================================================================================
  GROUP 53 — AI GM Rules: Creature Identity, Currency Standardization,
             Group Combat Simplification, Turn-Based Combat Enforcement,
             Character Creation Validation Gate
  Purpose: Resolve systemic GM AI failures identified in Testing.JSON playtest.
           Fix: generic creature names, "Crowns" currency confusion, multi-enemy
           tracking chaos, narrative-only combat bypassing mechanics, and players
           being able to abandon character creation mid-wizard.
================================================================================

  PROBLEM SET (identified from Testing.JSON audit):
    - GM AI was naming hostile NPCs just "Beast" with no creature identity
    - Currency used "Crowns" narratively but pc.gold stores GP; no conversion rule
    - Multi-enemy encounters described plural creatures but only one was tracked
    - Combat happened in narrative without encounterStarted; HP changes never applied
    - Players could press Escape or click X to close CharacterCreation.svelte mid-wizard
    - Character creation had no complete-all-steps gate at the close/exit paths

  --- FILE 1: src/lib/game/creature-templates.ts ---

  CREATURE_KEYWORDS table: Added a terminal fallback entry at the end of the array.
  Catches any creature named "Beast", "Monster", "Creature", "Entity", or "Fiend"
  that previously matched NOTHING, resulting in generic Strike/Slam from DEFAULT_ATTACKS.

    New entry (inserted before the closing bracket):
      { pattern: /\bbeast\b|\bmonster\b|\bcreature\b|\bfiend\b|\bentity\b/i,
        attacks: [
          { name: 'Claw', damageType: 'slashing' },
          { name: 'Bite', damageType: 'piercing' }
        ]
      }

  generateAbilities(): Added a new else-if branch for the same generic keywords
  so unidentified creatures get STR primary (+3), CON secondary (+2), DEX -1
  instead of all-10 baseline ability scores.

    New branch (after the wolf|snake|rat... branch):
      } else if (/\bbeast\b|\bmonster\b|\bcreature\b|\bentity\b/i.test(lower)) {
        abilities.str += 3;
        abilities.con += 2;
        abilities.dex = Math.max(8, abilities.dex - 1);
      }

  --- FILE 2: src/lib/game/gm-context.ts ---
  ALL CHANGES apply to buildNarrativeSystemPrompt(), buildSystemPrompt() (legacy),
  and buildStateExtractionPrompt().

  NARRATIVE PROMPT (buildNarrativeSystemPrompt):

  1. STARTING COMBAT section — added ALL COMBAT IS TURN-BASED rule:
     "ALL COMBAT IS TURN-BASED: If a player character is actively participating in
      a fight — attacking, defending, using abilities, or being targeted — the
      encounter MUST be started via encounterStarted with ALL relevant combatants
      listed. There is no such thing as a 'minor scuffle' that bypasses combat
      tracking. The ONLY exception is purely observational combat: a player
      character watching a battle from complete safety (a telescope, a hidden
      overlook, through a window) may receive pure narrative description. The moment
      the player character joins, intervenes, is targeted, or enters the area of
      conflict, encounterStarted MUST fire immediately."

  2. DURING COMBAT section — added GROUP COMBAT RULE:
     "GROUP COMBAT RULE: When multiple enemies are present in an encounter, only
      ONE creature actively engages the player character at a time — the lead
      creature steps forward while the others hang back, circle, or wait for an
      opening. Narrate a brief reason for this each round. If remaining creatures
      disengage after one is defeated, write a single clear narrative reason in one
      sentence. This keeps combat legible and prevents multi-enemy tracking confusion."

  3. New section: CREATURE NAMING (inserted after DIALOGUE & SOCIAL ENCOUNTERS):
     - NEVER use "Beast", "Monster", "Creature", or "Entity" as a creature's name
     - Always use a specific, descriptive identity: "Dire Wolf", "Corrupted Warg",
       "Mountain Cave Bear", "Alpha Timber Wolf", "Lab-Bred Houndfiend", etc.
     - Flavor prefixes encouraged: "Elder", "Alpha", "Cursed", "Great", "Shadow"
     - If an NPC was already named "Beast" in state, use npcChanges field "name"
       to rename it to a proper identity
     - The creature description field must describe appearance, not just repeat name

  4. New section: CURRENCY RULES (inserted after CREATURE NAMING):
     - Only Gold Pieces (gp), Silver Pieces (sp), Copper Pieces (cp) have
       mechanical value
     - World-flavor currency names ("Crowns", "Ducats", "Marks") = 1:1 with gp
     - goldChange entries ALWAYS use standard GP amounts
     - "50 Crowns" → goldChange delta: 50
     - Do NOT treat flavor currencies as worth more or less than gp unless
       adventure notes define an explicit conversion

  LEGACY PROMPT (buildSystemPrompt — YOU MUST NOT section):
    Added two new bullets to the YOU MUST NOT list:
    - "Use 'Beast', 'Monster', 'Creature', or any other generic label as a
       creature's name — always use a specific, descriptive identity"
    - "Start combat without firing encounterStarted regardless of how minor the
       fight seems — ALL player-involved combat uses the turn-based encounter system"

  ENCOUNTER DECLARATION DISCIPLINE section (legacy prompt):
    Added four new rules after the scouting/dialogue line:
    - ALL COMBAT IS TURN-BASED rule (mirrors narrative prompt)
    - GROUP COMBAT simplified rule (one enemy at a time; single-sentence exits)
    - CREATURE NAMING short rule
    - CURRENCY short rule

  STATE EXTRACTION PROMPT (buildStateExtractionPrompt):
    Added four new rules after the GOLD PAYMENTS line:
    - CURRENCY NORMALIZATION: all flavor currency names = 1:1 gp in goldChange
    - CREATURE NAMING: if NPC in state is named generically and narrative gives
      a specific identity, emit npcChanges field "name" to rename it
    - COMBAT TRACKING: if fight happened but no encounterStarted this turn, emit it
    - GROUP COMBAT: when enemies flee after partial defeat, emit npcChanges for them
      so they are not left in abandoned/limbo state

  --- FILE 3: src/lib/components/CharacterCreation.svelte ---

  CHARACTER CREATION LOCK — prevents closing the wizard before completing all steps.
  Character creation is mandatory; players cannot have a classless or incomplete
  character enter an adventure.

  Changes (3 locations + 1 CSS addition):

  1. handleKeydown() — Escape key no longer closes the modal:
     OLD: if (event.key === 'Escape') { isOpen = false; }
     NEW: if (event.key === 'Escape') { event.preventDefault(); }
          (with comment: "Character creation must be completed")

  2. Backdrop onclick — clicking outside the modal no longer closes it:
     OLD: onclick={(e) => { if (e.target === e.currentTarget) isOpen = false; }}
     NEW: onclick={(e) => { void e; /* backdrop click blocked */ }}

  3. Close button (✕) — now disabled with tooltip:
     OLD: <button type="button" class="close-btn"
               onclick={() => (isOpen = false)} aria-label="Close">✕</button>
     NEW: <button type="button" class="close-btn" disabled
               title="Complete character creation to continue"
               aria-label="Cannot close — character creation required">✕</button>

  4. CSS — added disabled style for .close-btn:
     .close-btn:disabled { opacity: 0.3; cursor: not-allowed; }

  The ONLY path that closes the modal remains the successful submitCharacter() call
  (isOpen = false after a 200 OK response from the server).

  Pre-existing errors in CharacterCreation.svelte (unrelated, unchanged):
    - 4× drag-drop div ARIA role warnings (a11y)
    - 2× -webkit-line-clamp CSS warnings
    - 1× empty .dragon-empty ruleset warning
    - 1× number | undefined type mismatch in AC preview calculation

  --- RESULTS ---
  svelte-check: 0 new errors introduced
    creature-templates.ts : 0 errors

Source: Testing.JSON playtest audit (17 bugs identified).

================================================================================
--- FILE 1: src/lib/game/gm-context.ts ---
================================================================================

  5 distinct changes across buildNarrativeSystemPrompt, buildSystemPrompt (legacy),
  buildStateExtractionPrompt, and formatCharacterBrief.

  ── CHANGE 1 (BUG-12): Inventory guard in buildNarrativeSystemPrompt YOU MUST NOT ──
  Added two new rules to the YOU MUST NOT section of the primary narrative prompt:

  NEW (after consumable items rule):
  - "Narrate a character using a weapon or armor they do not have in their
    inventory — if the Gear list is empty or lacks a weapon, the character is
    unarmed; narrate bare-hands or improvised weapon options, or suggest
    acquiring a weapon first"
  - "Assume a character has a class feature, proficiency, or spell if their
    class information is missing or classless — always check the PARTY section
    before granting class-specific mechanics"

  Purpose: Prevents GM hallucinating a battleaxe for a character with an empty
  inventory (as seen in test data where player was narrated swinging a battleaxe
  they never possessed).

  ── CHANGE 2 (BUG-12, legacy prompt YOU MUST NOT) ──
  Added matching rules to the legacy buildSystemPrompt's YOU MUST NOT section:
  - "Narrate a character using a weapon or armor they do not have in their
    inventory — if their Gear list is empty or lacks a suitable weapon, they
    are unarmed; present improvised weapon or bare-hand options, or suggest
    acquiring a weapon first"
  - "Assume class features or spells for a character whose class is shown as
    classless or not assigned"

  ── CHANGE 3 (BUG-11): Show classless characters correctly in character brief ──
  formatCharacterBrief() now shows "(classless — no class selected)" when
  c.classes.length === 0 instead of falling through to getPrimaryClass() which
  was returning 'fighter' by default, causing the GM to think the character was
  a fighter and grant them Proficiency / Fighting Style / etc.

  OLD:
    const classDesc = c.classes.length > 1
        ? c.classes.map((cl) => `${cl.name} ${cl.level}`).join('/')
        : getPrimaryClass(c);

  NEW:
    const classDesc = c.classes.length === 0
        ? '(classless — no class selected)'
        : c.classes.length > 1
            ? c.classes.map((cl) => `${cl.name} ${cl.level}`).join('/')
            : getPrimaryClass(c);

  ── CHANGE 4 (BUG-06): Fix contradicting encounterStarted rule in state extraction ──
  The buildStateExtractionPrompt had two contradicting rules:
    RULE A (IMPORTANT GUIDELINES): "COMBAT TRACKING: If narrative describes a fight
      but no encounterStarted was emitted this turn, you MUST emit encounterStarted"
    RULE B (IMPORTANT GUIDELINES): "COMBAT PROSE WITHOUT encounterStarted: If
      narrative contains combat phrases but no encounterStarted, do NOT retroactively
      emit encounterStarted — the narrative prose was written prematurely"

  RULE B was overriding RULE A and causing the state extractor to emit {} on
  combat turns, leaving encounters untracked (chain: no encounterStarted →
  no active encounter → no HP tracking, no XP, no initiative = BUG-06/07/08/10).

  OLD (RULE B verbatim):
  "COMBAT PROSE WITHOUT encounterStarted: If the narrative contains
  combat-declaration phrases ("Combat begins!", "Hostilities break out!") but no
  encounterStarted was included in this turn's stateChanges, do NOT retroactively
  emit encounterStarted — the narrative prose was written prematurely, and adding
  one now would create broken encounter state."

  NEW (RULE B corrected):
  "COMBAT PROSE WITHOUT encounterStarted: If the narrative shows that actual combat
  took place (enemies attacking, damage taken, characters fighting) but no
  encounterStarted was emitted in the stateChanges, you MUST emit encounterStarted
  with all enemies present — this is critical for encounter tracking. The ONLY
  exception: if the narrative contains ONLY a declaration phrase like "Combat
  begins!" without any actual fighting described, do not emit encounterStarted."

  ── CHANGE 5 (BUG-01): Expand COMBAT EXTRACTION RULES ──
  Added explicit instruction that combat turns are NOT exempt from extracting
  non-damage state changes. The AI was interpreting "do not invent damage numbers"
  as "return {} during combat" — leaving goldChange, questUpdates, itemsGained,
  conditionsApplied, etc. unextracted.

  ADDED (after existing "You may still extract..." line):
  "IMPORTANT: Even during a combat turn, you MUST still extract ALL non-attack
  state changes: goldChange (gold paid/received), questUpdates (quest completed/
  objectives done), itemsGained/Lost (loot picked up, items consumed),
  conditionsApplied, npcChanges (NPC dying, fleeing, disposition change),
  locationsAdded, sceneFactsAdded, and companionPromoted. Combat does NOT exempt
  you from extracting these. Returning {} during combat is almost always wrong."

  ── CHANGE 6 (BUG-03/15): Fix QUEST GOLD EXTRACTION over-suppression ──
  The existing QUEST GOLD EXTRACTION rule was suppressing ALL goldChange when a
  quest completed that turn — even when the quest had rewards.gold === 0 (empty
  rewards from BUG-02). This left gold unpaid from either distributeQuestRewards
  (which distributed 0) or from direct goldChange emission.

  OLD:
  "QUEST GOLD EXTRACTION: If the narrative describes an NPC paying the party an
  amount that matches a quest completion reward in this same turn, do NOT emit
  goldChange — the engine's distributeQuestRewards function already handles
  distributing that gold. Only emit goldChange for payments clearly separate from
  quest reward distribution."

  NEW:
  "QUEST GOLD EXTRACTION: If the narrative describes an NPC paying the party an
  amount that matches a quest completion reward AND that quest has a non-zero gold
  reward in this same turn, do NOT emit goldChange — the engine's
  distributeQuestRewards function already handles distributing that gold. However,
  if the completed quest had no gold reward (rewards.gold === 0) or if the gold
  payment is clearly separate from quest reward distribution, you MUST emit
  goldChange for that payment."

================================================================================
--- FILE 2: src/lib/server/ai/adventure-turn.ts ---
================================================================================

  2 changes: lastInteractionTurn scoping, quest rewards floor.

  ── CHANGE 7 (BUG-13): lastInteractionTurn scoped to party location ──
  The narrative-scan that updates npc.lastInteractionTurn was updating ALL NPCs
  whose name appeared anywhere in the narrative text — including distant NPCs
  that were merely mentioned in lore, backstory, or flashback narration. This
  caused wrong turn numbers (e.g., Darith.lastInteractionTurn = 23 when the last
  real interaction was turn 19).

  OLD (lines ~2565-2575):
    // Update lastInteractionTurn for NPCs mentioned by name in the narrative
    if (narrativeText) {
        const narrativeLower = narrativeText.toLowerCase();
        for (const npc of state.npcs) {
            const nameLower = npc.name.toLowerCase();
            const firstName = npc.name.split(/\s+/)[0].toLowerCase();
            if (narrativeLower.includes(nameLower) || (firstName.length >= 3 && narrativeLower.includes(firstName))) {
                npc.lastInteractionTurn = turnNumber;
            }
        }
    }

  NEW:
    // Update lastInteractionTurn for NPCs mentioned by name in the narrative.
    // Scoped to NPCs at the party's current location — prevents distant NPCs
    // that are merely referenced in lore or backstory from getting their
    // interaction timestamp bumped incorrectly (fixes BUG-13).
    if (narrativeText) {
        const narrativeLower = narrativeText.toLowerCase();
        // Collect NPCs already updated this turn via state changes (don't double-touch).
        const alreadyUpdatedThisTurn = new Set<string>(
            state.npcs.filter((n) => n.lastInteractionTurn === turnNumber).map((n) => n.id)
        );
        for (const npc of state.npcs) {
            if (alreadyUpdatedThisTurn.has(npc.id)) continue;
            // Only update NPCs physically present at the party's location.
            if (npc.locationId !== state.partyLocationId) continue;
            const nameLower = npc.name.toLowerCase();
            const firstName = npc.name.split(/\s+/)[0].toLowerCase();
            if (narrativeLower.includes(nameLower) || (firstName.length >= 3 && narrativeLower.includes(firstName))) {
                npc.lastInteractionTurn = turnNumber;
            }
        }
    }

  ── CHANGE 8 (BUG-02/15): Quest rewards minimum XP floor at creation ──
  When quests were created with {xp:0, gold:0} (AI failing to populate rewards),
  distributeQuestRewards() returned immediately without distributing anything —
  making quest completion feel unrewarding and leaving players without XP/gold.

  Fixed by adding a floor guard immediately after the Quest object is constructed
  in the questsAdded processing block of applyGMStateChanges():

  ADDED (after quest object construction, before state.quests.push()):
    // BUG-02/15 guard: if the AI emitted empty rewards ({xp:0,gold:0}), apply a
    // level-appropriate XP floor so distributeQuestRewards always has something to
    // distribute when the quest completes.
    if (quest.rewards.xp === 0 && quest.rewards.gold === 0) {
        quest.rewards.xp = Math.max(50, (quest.recommendedLevel ?? 1) * 100);
        console.warn(`[questsAdded] "${quest.name}" had empty rewards (xp=0,gold=0) — auto-set xp=${quest.rewards.xp}`);
    }

  The condition is both-zero to avoid changing intentional 0-gold quests that
  still have XP, or 0-XP acknowledgement quests that have gold.

GROUP 55 — FEATS TAB + AUTO-QUIVER FOR RANGED CHARACTERS
