--- FEATS TAB IN ADVENTURE STATUS PANEL ---

  File: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

  Added a "Feats" section to the Status tab of the adventure journal panel.
  - Appears between Hit Dice and Skills sections
  - Conditionally renders only when pc.feats.length > 0
  - Each feat renders as a skill-chip with a distinct purple/lavender accent
    (.feat-chip style: rgba(200,160,255,...) background/border, #c8a0ff text)
  - Chip label: ✦ <displayName> from FeatDefinition (falls back to fmt(name))
  - Chip tooltip (native title=): full feat description text from FEATS data
  - Uses getFeat(name) imported from '$lib/game' (via data/feats.ts → data/index.ts)

  Also fixed pre-existing a11y errors in ctx-menu div (GROUP 54 code):
  - Added tabindex="-1" to role="menu" div
  - Added onkeydown handler alongside onclick

--- AUTO-QUIVER FOR RANGED WEAPON STARTERS ---

  File: src/lib/game/character-creation.ts

  After the automatic belt/coin-purse injection block, added a parallel block
  that checks whether the character's starting inventory includes a bow or
  crossbow (weapons with 'ammunition' property; sling and blowgun excluded
  because they use non-quiver ammo types).

  Logic:
    const hasQuiver = allBuilt.some(i => containerType === 'quiver')
    If !hasQuiver:
      const needsQuiver = allBuilt.some(weapon => 
        (simple-ranged | martial-ranged) && properties.includes('ammunition')
        && name !== 'sling' && name !== 'blowgun')
      If needsQuiver → push a new ContainerItem of containerType 'quiver'
        (same isStartingEquipment: true pattern as belt/coin-purse)

  Effect: Existing Pass 2 ammo routing at line 1259+ already sends arrows/bolts
  to the quiver if one is present. Auto-injection ensures rangers, fighters
  with bows, rogues with hand-crossbows, etc. always have a quiver available
  from the start. Sling bullets and blowgun needles continue to route to
  backpack or belt pouch as before.

  Weapons that trigger quiver injection:
    shortbow, longbow, light-crossbow, hand-crossbow, heavy-crossbow

  Weapons that do NOT trigger quiver injection:
    dart (thrown, no ammunition property), sling, blowgun, net

================================================================================
GROUP 56 — PROFICIENCY SECTIONS + CLOTHING AUTO-EQUIP + URCHIN TOKEN + VESTMENTS

--- PROFICIENCY SUBDIVISION IN ADVENTURE STATUS PANEL ---

  File: src/lib/components/JournalPanel.svelte

  Replaced the single "Other Proficiencies" section with three distinct sections:

  1. ARMOR PROFICIENCIES — uses pc.armorProficiencies
     Displays: Light Armor, Medium Armor, Heavy Armor, Shields

  2. WEAPON PROFICIENCIES — uses pc.weaponProficiencies with deduplication
     Deduplication: if 'simple' is present, all individual simple weapon names
     are hidden; if 'martial' is present, all individual martial weapon names
     are hidden. This prevents redundant entries for classes like Rogue that
     list both 'simple' and then specific individual weapons.

     SIMPLE_WEAPON_NAMES set: club, dagger, greatclub, handaxe, javelin,
       light-hammer, mace, quarterstaff, sickle, spear, dart, light-crossbow,
       shortbow, sling, unarmed
     MARTIAL_WEAPON_NAMES set: battleaxe, flail, glaive, greataxe, greatsword,
       halberd, lance, longsword, maul, morningstar, pike, rapier, scimitar,
       shortsword, trident, war-pick, warhammer, whip, blowgun, hand-crossbow,
       heavy-crossbow, longbow, net

     dedupedWeaponProfs() function added to filter the proficiency list.

  3. TOOLS & VEHICLES — uses pc.toolProficiencies
     Displays: thieves' tools, herbalism kit, artisan's tools, musical instruments,
     navigator's tools, disguise kit, forgery kit, poisoner's kit, gaming sets,
     Land Vehicles, Water Vessels.

  PROF_DISPLAY expanded from 6 to ~50 entries covering all individual weapon
  names, all tool/kit keys, and vehicle types.

  PROF_TOOLTIPS expanded to include tooltips for all new PROF_DISPLAY keys.

  "Vehicles Land" renamed to "Land Vehicles" game-wide:
    - PROF_DISPLAY key 'vehicles-land' now maps to 'Land Vehicles'
    - PROF_TOOLTIPS entry for 'vehicles-land' updated accordingly

--- MISCITEM EQUIPPED FIELD ---

  File: src/lib/game/types.ts

  Added optional field to MiscItem interface:
    equipped?: boolean;
  Allows clothing and other wearable misc items to be tracked as
  worn/equipped vs stored in backpack.

--- CLOTHING AUTO-EQUIP SYSTEM ---

  File: src/lib/game/character-creation.ts

  New constant: CLOTHING_ITEM_DATA
    Placed before CONTAINER_NAME_MAP. Maps lowercase clothing names to:
      { weight, value (gp), description, rank }
    Rank determines priority when choosing which set to auto-equip:
      Rank 6: vestments, priest vestments
      Rank 5: fine clothes, noble clothes
      Rank 4: traveler's clothes, travelers clothes
      Rank 3: robes, costume, 2 costumes, costume clothes, dark common clothes,
               dark common clothes with a hood, dark clothes
      Rank 2: common clothes (fallback default)

  itemFromLabel() modification:
    At the TOP of itemFromLabel (before container check), normalises baseName
    to lowercase and checks against CLOTHING_ITEM_DATA. If matched, returns
    a MiscItem with:
      category: 'misc', tags: ['clothing'], equipped: false
      + correct weight, value, description, and spaceTaken from CLOTHING_ITEM_DATA

  Auto-equip block added after the weapon auto-equip block, before Pass 2:
    - Finds all items in allBuilt where category === 'misc' and tags includes 'clothing'
    - If NONE found: injects a new 'Common Clothes' item with equipped: true
    - If found: sorts by rank (highest first); sets sorted[0].equipped = true,
      all others equipped: false. Unequipped clothing routes to backpack via Pass 2.

  Misc fallback updated:
    - description: 'A personal item carried as starting equipment: .'
      (was: 'Starting equipment: .')
    - weight: 0.1 (was: 0)

--- URCHIN BACKGROUND: TOKEN ITEM ---

  File: src/lib/game/data/backgrounds.ts

  The urchin background has a 'parentToken' choice. Previously this created
  a fixed item named "Token to Remember Your Parents By" regardless of input.

  New behaviour:
    - itemNameTemplate: '{parentToken}' — item is named exactly what the player
      typed (e.g. "Worn Pearl", "Cracked Locket", "Faded Portrait")
    - description (from misc fallback): 'A personal item carried as starting
      equipment: <typed name>.'
    - prompt updated to ask for the item name (max 6 words) rather than a description
    - placeholder: 'e.g. Worn Pearl, Cracked Locket...'

--- VESTMENTS (ACOLYTE BACKGROUND) ---

  No change to backgrounds.ts required. The acolyte background always included
  'Vestments' as equipment. With the new CLOTHING_ITEM_DATA system, calling
  itemFromLabel('Vestments') now creates a proper MiscItem with:
    weight: 3, value: 1 gp, rank: 6
    tags: ['clothing']
    description: 'Priestly garments of religious service worn by acolytes and
      clergy during worship and travel.'
  Auto-equip selects vestments over common clothes due to higher rank.
  Common clothes (also in the acolyte kit) goes to backpack.
